yet feryd terrible ferefull iudgementes nat affrayde moost abhominable synnes presence sight god cum ye creature god let v vtterly distroy person holly fully gyue iniury vnto lord thou erthe doest moche dyscrete hyr selfe moche dyd nat presume thynge vnto hyr selfe famylyarely taught holy goost durst nat absteyne one hole day refection except surely rauysshed rapte vp aboue hyr selfe hyr sensys yet sumtyme whan rapte dyd attempte proue take hyr refection auoide thoccasion murmure person hyr company meanes myght receyue hyr stomack payne therof sumtyme almoost ouercum therfore afterwarde lyberty absteyne whan wold non occasion taken therof man durst aske heribid ca dyd also oftentymes whan preest lyfted vp blessyd sacrament body lorde aboue hed se bytwyxte handes preest forme shap moost fayre chylde also se great multitude aungels descendyng heuyn great lyght vsynge receyuynge sacrament se spirite lorde remaynynge soule preste lyghtenynge meruelouse clerenes el yf preest receyuyd body lorde vnworthely se lord departed soule indignacion leuynge great darkenes voyde goodnes pthe gyfte strengthe gyuen man feruent remembraunce christes passion xii chapitre deuoute ofte remembraunce passion lorde also gyuen vnto man gyft gostly strength agaynste spyrytuall enemy multitude temptacions gyfte inordinate feare put away hardy inordynate boldnes reduced due measure aduersities ben strongly borne suffred euer crucified christe thrugh feruent remembraunce blessyd passion animated strengthed entrepryse great harde thynges contempne set nought worldly pleasure suffre paciently gladly tribulacions expugne ouercum vyces faythefull seruaunt whiche doeth feruently remembre lordes passion lorde hathe gyuen many grace person say doeth consydre se meruelouse incomprehensible strengthe christe interprysyng great battels sufferaunce vanquesshynge subduynge deuyll say entreprysynge great harde thynges faught great terryble battelles saluacion enemy vnkynde man also meruelouse strengthe christe doeth appere pacience suffred obprobriouse sharpe greuouse tourmentes creature thyrdely incomprehensible strengthe shewed subduynge myghty strong lorde rather may saye tyraunte deuyll vsurped dominion ouer worlde whome lorde dethe crosse strongely dyd ouercum dethe destrued autor cause deth thynges well considered maruell yf faythefull knyght christe folower lorde moued example christe entrepryse go aboute great harde thynges harde vyle paynefull thynges gladly diligently feruently wyll attempte specyally yf laude honour god helthe conforte soules nothyng harde vyle paynfull hym suffre god whiche dyd great thynges hym vyle wretche yea also thynketh thynges though neuer paynefull swete pleasaunt delectable commendable moche desyred yf thereby may assimulate made lyke vnto moost shamefull paynefull dethe christe lorde god thynges faythfull seruant doeth gladly occupieth hym selfe aiudiously thynges sercheth oft remembreth desyreth fulfyll feruent mynde nat grudgynge sayenge put vyle offyce shame labour payne rather thynkynge shal nat thynges glad mynde doeth nat repute thynke hym selfe reputacion serueth god thynketh greate thynge wolde please almighty god onely goodnes accept vnto seruyce vyle vnworthy moost myserable wretche wherefore thynges herte onely pleased may conformable lorde god doeth folow hym sufferaunce trouble moche may hys frailtie suffreth knowledgeth synnes ioye lorde honoured glad pacience sufferaunce tribulacions faythfull seruaunte hathe strongly subdued tyed appetyte vnder yocke captiuitie ryght reason shall nat haue wanton pleasure carnall worldly desyre yet vayne vnprofytable thynge also kepeth herte diligence castell greate strengthe wyll nat suffre synfull thought rest therein yet vayne vnfruitfull imaginacions wandre therein euer thynkynge considerynge thynges ben spyrytuall godly inducyng vnto god great ioye desyreth thinges feruently laboureth bryng effect moche lyfe euermore moost parte chaffe myxt corne therfore faythfull seruant taketh rydell wyndose discrecion hande wyndeth purgeth chaffe corne doore herte taketh hande burnynge sharpe swerde kepe diligently herte paradyse god euer herte desyreth eate tree lyfe suche thoughtes godlye spirituall lyuely suche diligentely doeth cheryssh nourysshe yf thoughte onely loke vnto fruyte forboden thynge contrary commaundementes pleasure god suche thoughtes wyll shortely expell frome herte shall haue pleasaunt abydynge dysceytfull serpent shall haue none entraunce herte ne yet flatterynge persuacion woman yf peraduenture perceyue suche appere herte anon wyll remoue wyth indignacion sharpe rebuke onely bene nourysshed manly godlye vertuouse thoughtes therefore suche persone thus puryfyed soule bodye may trewly order hym selfe contemplacyon god neuer lyfteth vppe syght iyes vnto vayne thynges ne hys eares heare noysome vnprofytable thynges hys nose smell swete odour smelles hys mouthe taste delycate thynges ne yet hys touchynge feele softe thynges inordynately dylygence kepeth hym selfe bothe inwardely outwardly nowe shoulde nat called seruaunte bounde rather lorde free hathe domynyon ouer hym selfe subdewynge inordynate sensuall appetytes muche man may haue lordeshyppe ouer hym selfe thys lyfe say suche persone puritie mooste apte receyue godlye influencys spyrytuall illustracions sonne iustyce doeth inhabyte suche pure clene soule shynynge euery corner thereof lyghtenynge inwarde partes thre power soule may thynges necessarye saluacion power father almyghty knoweth thynges wysdome sonne sauyoure christe iesus wyll goodthynges goodnes hooly gooste thre mansyons tabernacle god maketh soule iuste pure persone fyndeth nothynge shulde let resyste contrarye hym lorde doeth shyne remayneth good men conueniently set ryght hand theyr death ware founde ryght part hauynge charitie good workes euyll men also conuenietly set left hande wolde nat folow ryght parte doyng good werkes ye loue god tho lefte part loue temporall vayne thynges tho ryght parte loue eternall thynges shall christe recounte remembre werkes mercy vnto good men ryght hande whiche dyd christe membres shal say
